class=\"row\">\n  \t<div class=\"col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12 col-xs-12\">\n      <h1 class=\"title\">\n\t  \t  <!-- #BeginEditable \"Category-Name\" -->\n    Lyrics for Boy Scouts Songs, Girl Scouts Songs, and American Patriotic Songs\n\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n      </h1>\n      <!-- #BeginEditable \"Category-Description\" -->\n\n                <p class=\"mobile-text hidden-xs\">This songbook was created for everyone who has ever been involved in Scouting. It is a compilation of camp songs that are popular at Scout camps around the country. There are <a href=\"/categories/action-songs.html\">action song lyrics</a> to keep you moving, <a href=\"/categories/patriotic-songs.html\" title=\"Patriotic Songs\">Patriotic Song lyrics</a>, <a href=\"/categories/boy-scout-songs.html\" title=\"Boy Scout Songs\">Boy Scout song lyrics</a> and <a href=\"/categories/girl-scout-songs.html\" title=\"Girl Scout Songs\">Girl Scout song lyrics</a> that have been sung by Boy Scouts and Girl Scouts for generations.</p>\n                <p class=\"mobile-text hidden-xs\">If you are currently a Boy Scout, Girl Scout, or Scouter, I hope that your visit here will inspire you with new songs for your meeting, campfire, or summer camp visit.</p>\n                <p class=\"mobile-text hidden-xs\">If you were a Boy or Girl Scout but are no longer active, I hope that your visit here will bring back fond memories of the fun times that you had singing around the campfire or on the trail  with your friends.</p>\n\n                <!-- #EndEditable
